 jaane kin baton kaa rakhte hue karen puja
 
 
 1
 puja ke din sabase pehle ek badi or saaf chaowkee par laal yaa pilaa kapadaa bicha kar uske uparalakshmi-ganeshaki murtiyon sthapit rakh den
 Keep in mind that they should be facing east or west

 2
 pujan karne vaale sabhi log murtiyon ke saamne kii taraf baithen
 3
 ab ek kalash ko lakshmi ke paas chawlon par rakhen
 Wrap a coconut in a red cloth on the urn in such a way that the face of the coconut is visible
 3
 This urn is the symbol of Varuna
 kalash ke paas do bade deepak rakhen jisamen ek ghi kaa or doosraa tel kaa deepak ho
 Place one lamp to the right of the outpost and the other at the feet of the idols
 ek deepakganesh jike paas rakhen
 4
 murtiyon vaali chaowkee ke saamne choti chaowkee rakhkar us par laal vastra bichhaaen
 Draw a fist with rice on the red cloth on the Kalash to symbolize the Navagraha
 5
 Draw sixteen symbols of rice towards Ganeshji which are considered to be the symbol of the mother
 navagraha or shodash maatrakaa ke bich swastik kaa chihn banaaen
 6
 ab iske bich main supaari rakhen
 In front of the small outpost, fill three plates and the vase with water
 7
